Wolfgang,
I applied all of these patches to a standard 2.0.30
kernel source tree (NOT a Red Hat one). The ncr* patches have
to be applied one at a time. I've also added in my .config
file, put it into your /usr/src/linux* directory and make config
(not changing anything) followed by a make dep and a make clean.

Dave
